Question Exam AWS Certified Security - Specialty topic 1 question 177 discussion:<br>A Security Engineer creates an Amazon S3 bucket policy that denies access to all users. A few days later, the Security Engineer adds an additional statement to the bucket policy to allow read-only access to one other employee. Even after updating the policy, the employee still receives an access denied message.<br>What is the likely cause of this access denial?<br><br>[Discussion](https://www.examtopics.com/discussions/amazon/view/30027-exam-aws-certified-security-specialty-topic-1-question-177/)<br><br>A. The ACL in the bucket needs to be updated<br>B. The IAM policy does not allow the user to access the bucket<br>C. It takes a few minutes for a bucket policy to take effect<br>D. The allow permission is being overridden by the deny<br><br>Question Exam AWS Certified Security - Specialty topic 1 question 172 discussion:<br>A Security Engineer has launched multiple Amazon EC2 instances from a private AMI using an AWS CloudFormation template. AWS currently does not have sufficient capacity in the Region<br><br>Question Exam AWS Certified Security - Specialty topic 1 question 178 discussion:<br>A company plans to use custom AMIs to launch Amazon EC2 instances across multiple AWS accounts in a single Region to perform security monitoring and analytics tasks. The EC2 instances are launched in EC2 Auto Scaling groups. To increase the security of the solution, a Security Engineer will manage the lifecycle of the custom AMIs in a centralized account and will encrypt them with a centrally managed AWS KMS CMK. The Security Engineer configured the KMS key policy to allow cross-account access. However, the EC2 instances are still not being properly launched by the EC2 Auto Scaling groups.<br>Which combination of configuration steps should the Security Engineer take to ensure the EC2 Auto Scaling groups have been granted the proper permissions to execute tasks?<br><br>[Discussion](https://www.examtopics.com/discussions/amazon/view/51573-exam-aws-certified-security-specialty-topic-1-question-178/)<br><br>A. Create a customer-managed CMK in the centralized account. Allow other applicable accounts to use that key for cryptographical operations by applying proper cross-account permissions in the key policy. Create an IAM role in all applicable accounts and configure its access policy to allow the use of the centrally managed CMK for cryptographical operations. Configure EC2 Auto Scaling groups within each applicable account to use the created IAM role to launch EC2 instances.<br>B. Create a customer-managed CMK in the centralized account. Allow other applicable accounts to use that key for cryptographical operations by applying proper cross-account permissions in the key policy. Create an IAM role in all applicable accounts and configure its access policy with permissions to create grants for the centrally managed CMK. Use this IAM role to create a grant for the centrally managed CMK with permissions to perform cryptographical operations and with the EC2 Auto Scaling service-linked role defined as the grantee principal.<br>C. Create a customer-managed CMK or an AWS managed CMK in the centralized account. Allow other applicable accounts to use that key for cryptographical operations by applying proper cross-account permissions in the key policy. Use the CMK administrator to create a CMK grant that includes permissions to perform cryptographical operations that define EC2 Auto Scaling service-linked roles from all other accounts as the grantee principal.<br>D. Create a customer-managed CMK or an AWS managed CMK in the centralized account. Allow other applicable accounts to use that key for cryptographical operations by applying proper cross-account permissions in the key policy. Modify the access policy for the EC2 Auto Scaling roles to perform cryptographical operations against the centrally managed CMK.<br><br>Question Exam AWS Certified Security - Specialty topic 1 question 179 discussion:<br>An organization wants to log all AWS API calls made within all of its AWS accounts, and must have a central place to analyze these logs.<br>What steps should be taken to meet these requirements in the MOST secure manner? DNS validation requires the domain to be hosted on Amazon Route 53.<br>B. Automatic renewal for domain validation requires the domain to be hosted on Amazon Route 53.<br>C. The domain has Certification Authority Authorization (CAA) DNS records that allow only specific certificate authorities.<br>D. DNS validation requires a TXT record instead of a CNAME record.<br><br>Question Exam AWS Certified Security - Specialty topic 1 question 428 discussion:<br>A security engineer is configuring a mechanism to send an alert when three or more failed sign-in attempts to the AWS Management Console occur during a 5-minute period. Use this new key to encrypt the snapshot in us-west-1.<br>C. Create an IAM policy that allows access to the customer managed key in us-east-1. Specify arn:aws:kms:us-west-1as the principal.<br>D. Create an IAM policy that allows access to the customer managed key in us-east-1. Specify arn:aws:rds:us-west-1 :* as the principal.<br><br>Question Exam AWS Certified Security - Specialty topic 1 question 488 discussion:<br>A company's application uses standard tier secure string parameters from AWS Systems Manager Parameter Store. To increase the security of the solution, a Security Engineer will manage the lifecycle of the custom AMIs in a centralized account and will encrypt them with a centrally managed AWS KMS CMK. The Security Engineer configured the KMS key policy to allow cross-account access. However, the EC2 instances are still not being properly launched by the EC2 Auto Scaling groups.<br>Which combination of configuration steps should the Security Engineer take to ensure the EC2 Auto Scaling groups have been granted the proper permissions to execute task?<br><br>[Discussion](https://www.examtopics.com/discussions/amazon/view/46551-exam-aws-certified-security-specialty-topic-1-question-178/)<br><br>A. Create a customer-managed CMK in the centralized account. Allow other applicable accounts to use that key for cryptographical operations by applying proper cross-account permissions in the key policy. Create an IAM role in all applicable accounts and configure its access policy to allow the use of the centrally managed CMK for cryptographical operations. Configure EC2 Auto Scaling groups within each applicable account to use the created IAM role to launch EC2 instances.<br>B. Create a customer-managed CMK in the centralized account. Allow other applicable accounts to use that key for cryptographical operations by applying proper cross-account permissions in the key policy. Create an IAM role in all applicable accounts and configure its access policy with permissions to create grants for the centrally managed CMK. Use this IAM role to create a grant for the centrally managed CMK with permissions to perform cryptographical operations and with the EC2 Auto Scaling service-linked role defined as the grantee principal.<br>C. Create a customer-managed CMK or an AWS managed CMK in the centralized account. Allow other applicable accounts to use that key for cryptographical operations by applying proper cross-account permissions in the key policy. Use the CMK administrator to create a CMK grant that includes permissions to perform cryptographical operations that define EC2 Auto Scaling service-linked roles from all other accounts as the grantee principal.<br>D. Create a customer-managed CMK or an AWS managed CMK in the centralized account. Allow other applicable accounts to use that key for cryptographical operations by applying proper cross-account permissions in the key policy. Modify the access policy for the EC2 Auto Scaling roles to perform cryptographical operations against the centrally managed CMK.<br><br>Question Exam AWS Certified Security - Specialty topic 1 question 182 discussion:<br>A company has hundreds of AWS accounts, and a centralized Amazon S3 bucket used to collect AWS CloudTrail logs for all of these accounts. A Security<br>Engineer wants to create a solution that will enable the company to run ad hoc queries against its CloudTrail logs dating back 3 years from when the trails were first enabled in the company's AWS account.<br>How should the company accomplish this with the least amount of administrative overhead?<br><br>[Discussion](https://www.examtopics.com/discussions/amazon/view/46743-exam-aws-certified-security-specialty-topic-1-question-182/)<br><br>A. Run an Amazon EMR cluster that uses a MapReduce job to examine the CloudTrail trails.<br>B. Use the events history feature of the CloudTrail console to query the CloudTrail trails.<br>C. Write an AWS Lambda function to query the CloudTrail trails. Configure the Lambda function to be executed whenever a new file is created in the CloudTrail S3 bucket.<br>D. Create an Amazon Athena table that looks at the S3 bucket the CloudTrail trails are being written to. Use Athena to run queries against the trails.<br><br>
